S  -> SUB PRE | SUB PRE OBJ | SUB PRE PEL | SUB PRE OBJ PEL | SUB PRE KET | SUB PRE OBJ KET | SUB PRE PEL KET | SUB PRE OBJ PEL KET
SUB -> FNOM | PRP | NN | NNP
PRE -> VB | JJ | FVERB
OBJ ->  NN | FNOM
PEL -> NN | JJ | FNOM | FADJE | FPREP
KET -> FPREP
FNOM -> NN VB | NN NN | NN PR | NN PRP | NN NN PR | NN NN | NN JJ | CD NN | NN JJ PR | NNP NNP | CD CD | CD NND | NND NN |  CD NND NN | NN CC NN | FNOM PRP | NNP CC NNP
FVERB -> SC VB | MD VB | VB VB | MD RB VB | NEG VB | VB JJ | NN VB
FADJE -> JJ RB | JJ NN | NN JJ| JJ JJ | JJ VB | NEG JJ | RB JJ
FPREP -> IN FPREP |IN NN | IN NN NN | IN NN IN | NN CD NN | NNP NNP | IN NNP
